# Comments for Question 3, LLM=Claude 3.5 Haiku

== Grader: Claude 3.7 Sonnet ==
  * grade_story_0.txt (grade=7.3)
    The pattern recognition center creates an effective backdrop for the scientific discovery narrative. The stained glass lamp serves as both physical object and symbolic conduit, cleverly connecting to the communication breakthrough through light patterns. The underwater setting is evoked through acoustic sensors and signals, creating a dual-environment tension. However, sensory details beyond visual elements are limited, missing opportunities for a more immersive atmosphere.

  * grade_story_105.txt (grade=7.3)

However, the "witch's flying carpet garage" feels disconnected from the main setting and insufficiently integrated into the world-building.
